```
- [x] Reviewed
  - ID: `CCP-501`
  - Status: `reviewed`
  - Task ID: `CCP-501`
  - Parent prompt ID: none
  - Batch prompt IDs: none
  - Source document: `docs/audits/PERFORMANCE_SCALABILITY_AUDIT_2026-03-30.md`

  - Created by: `Claude`
  - Created at: `2026-03-30T22:00:00Z`
  - Started at: `2026-03-31T00:53:27.587Z`
  - Claude used: yes
  - Review outcome: passed
  - Review issues: none
  - Reviewed at: `2026-04-01T18:12:28.957Z`
  - Reviewed by: `Codex`
  - Review method: `full-review`
  - Review scope: re-review after missing provenance
  - Execution target: `Claude Code`
  - Completed at: `2026-03-31T00:54:54.814Z`
  - Manual checklist:
    - [ ] First sync (clear localStorage lastSyncedAt): push sends ALL records, pull fetches ALL records
    - [ ] Second sync: push sends only records changed since last sync, pull requests only ?since=timestamp
```

```
    - [ ] scheduleNext(5, false) → {newLevel:4, nextDueAt: ~2 weeks} (floor at max(1, level-1))
    - [ ] gradeMove('Nf3','Nf3') → 'correct'; gradeMove('e4','Nf3') → 'incorrect'
    - [ ] createDrillSession: correct move → feedback='correct'; 3 wrong → feedback='showAnswer'
    - [ ] buildReviewSession returns only sequences with due positions, sorted by earliest nextDueAt
    - [ ] extractMainline returns TrainableSequence with correct moves/sans/fens from tree
    - [ ] All modules are pure: no IDB imports, no DOM, no Snabbdom
```
